The front office staff is terrific! Organized, professional and communicative along with caring and compassionate.

The office is so pleasant and really beautiful. They have an awesome screen on a wall in the waiting room with calming images flowing past. Love it!

The dental assistants are very knowledgeable, highly skilled, efficient and kind. And I really appreciated that I can always reach someone if I have a question or concern.

The hygienists are truly talented. I used to be a really nervous person when it came to getting my teeth cleaned but here I've had nothing but such positive experiences...great relief!

Obviously I highly recommend Dr Ross's dental practice. It's a warm, positive environment with great dental care across the spectrum from regular hygiene to those more difficult dental challenges!</Text>

Last week, I was kindly informed (re: warned) that my 2018 tags for my license plate were missing.  Helpful tip, slice that sucker up with a razor blade to avoid having yours stolen too and you won't have to go through this special purgatory.

So, I get a correctable violation and decide I'll just go before work on Monday morning.  I show up about 20-25 minutes before they open and I'm 8th in line; not bad, right?  Well, about 10 minutes before they open, our line (now around 30 people) get split into ID requests and registration requests.  Of course, ID requests get invited in first, so I've moved from 8th to 20 something in line.  Annoying, but they just opened, so whatever, I'll be ok.

I get to the front of the line and explain I need new tags for my car.  Here's where is gets interesting, and by interesting I mean ridiculous.  I am given number BB0004. The only reason I have this place a star, is the people working there weren't awful. <Review>Went out to the beach to have some beers and get something to eat and my wife had this place booked marked so we gave it a try. The staff was friendly and the view was great. When you can have a cold beer and overlook the doc it's always a good time. We looked over the menu and heard the daily specials and placed our order.

Shishito Peppers - These were very good that are drizzled with a brown sugar-soy glaze, sriracha, sesame and lime. Just because you hear peppers don't think mouth on fire but more of a tiny spice and great snack.

Royale with cheese - proprietary blend burger, aged white cheddar, LTO, housemade dill pickles, comeback sauce, kennebec chips, housemade ketchup. Burger was tender and juicy and had great flavor. It was a nice tasting burger.

Jidori chicken & waffles - vadouvan-spiced fried chicken, vanilla bean waffles, herb-infused maple syrup. This was a little different then your typical chicken and waffles. The vanilla bean waffles were a little different but had a good flavor and the boneless chicken thighs were golden brown with a  good crunch to it. The chicken also had good seasoning that complimented the syrup at every bite.

Good food with a view try this place out. I think you will bot be disappointed. Stay hungry my friends!</Review>< Gmap_id>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures>< review>
Took friends to the Pier yesterday on our #tenthousandstepsperday walk - and found this gem just by chance. Loved to sit outside and had a little bite. We tried family style - shared a lot- and loved every thing we tasted.

As I would be perfectly willing to make a detour and go with friends again, I give it five stars. If you are curious enough who I rate, please read on :-)

Thanks for reading my comment. Now, if you are curious enough about my "rating scheme", here's "the moment of truth. I am a music photographer who travels the world with the worlds greatest musical talents (Michael Jackson, AC/DC, Rolling Stones or Rammstein, to name a few) for almost 40 years. When being asked "where do you live" I tended to ask "in hotels". At my peak, I "shot" 250 shows a year. Will say: been there, saw and tasted it, and a lot, as I may say and much to the dismay of my doctor who is in my back to lose a few pounds. Quite a few, as I may add, which is why my wife and I walk ten thousand steps per day, where- and whenever we can - and explore a lot of new exciting places - places you may oversee when just driving by.

While I love to share my experience with others, I am sometimes shocked how people use their "power of word" to down-rate amazing places because of minor incidents (in my all time favourite‚Äã restaurant Le Petit Four on Sunset Plaza the owner was even called a racist as he refused to toast the (free) bread in his packed restaurant - they simply do not offer toasted bread, as no French‚Äã place does, as I may add). Or I just read "Chicken piccata so over-salted I hope the dog enjoys the leftovers tomorrow, I brought home most of the dish." Did they speak to their service? How could the restaurant learn that something was wrong when patrons even have their leftovers‚Äã boxed to take home? As a dog owner,‚Äã I want to take the writer and shake him or her really bad and say "you give over-salted food to your dog? Anyone with a bit of brain understands this is a horrible idea...‚Äã I hope you agree.

So If I had the say on this portal, I would offer just to see ratings of my friends. So I would see what the ratings were by like-minded people. Sadly, I have no say. I try not to compare apples with oranges. A place like this simply does not compare to "The Ritz". At first,‚Äã I assume that a restaurant is clean, they do not greet you with a gun - and they deliver whatever they promise. I do not give stars for things that are expected. In my rating scheme, three or more stars are awarded if they actually exceeded my expectation. Four, if I am sure I will come back. To achieve five stars, I must be willing to take a detour of thirty minutes or more to go again.

Thank you for reading this.<//review>
